### 1. [SPIRAL: Symbolic LLM Planning via Grounded and Reflective Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.23167)

**Type**: new

#### Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) often falter at complex planning tasks that require exploration and self-correction, as their linear reasoning process struggles to recover from early mistakes. While search algorithms like Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS) can explore alternatives, they are often ineffecti...

### 2. [AKG kernel Agent: A Multi-Agent Framework for Cross-Platform Kernel Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.23424)

**Authors**: Jinye Du, Quan Yuan, Zuyao Zhang, Yanzhi Yi, Jiahui Hu, Wangyi Chen, Yiyang Zhu, Qishui Zheng, Wenxiang Zou, Xiangyu Chang, Zuohe Zheng, Zichun Ye, Chao Liu, Shanni Li, Renwei Zhang, Yiping Deng, Xinwei Hu, Xuefeng Jin, Jie Zhao

#### Abstract

### 3. [Agent2World: Learning to Generate Symbolic World Models via Adaptive Multi-Agent Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.22336)

**Authors**: Mengkang Hu, Bowei Xia, Yuran Wu, Ailing Yu, Yude Zou, Qiguang Chen, Shijian Wang, Jiarui Jin, Kexin Li, Wenxiang Jiao, Yuan Lu, Ping Luo  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-31  
**Score**: 6.5  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.22336v1  

#### Abstract
Symbolic world models (e.g., PDDL domains or executable simulators) are central to model-based planning, but training LLMs to generate such world models is limited by the lack of large-scale verifiable supervision. Current approaches rely primarily on static validation methods that fail to catch beh...

### 4. [Replay Failures as Successes: Sample-Efficient Reinforcement Learning for Instruction Following](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.23457)

**Authors**: Kongcheng Zhang, Qi Yao, Shunyu Liu, Wenjian Zhang, Min Cen, Yang Zhou, Wenkai Fang, Yiru Zhao, Baisheng Lai, Mingli Song  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-31  
**Score**: 6.5  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.23457v1  

#### Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) has shown promise for aligning Large Language Models (LLMs) to follow instructions with various constraints. Despite the encouraging results, RL improvement inevitably relies on sampling successful, high-quality responses; however, the initial model often struggles to gen...

### 5. [InSPO: Unlocking Intrinsic Self-Reflection for LLM Preference Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.23126)

**Authors**: Yu Li, Tian Lan, Zhengling Qi  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-31  
**Score**: 6.0  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.23126v1  

#### Abstract
Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) and its variants have become standard for aligning Large Language Models due to their simplicity and offline stability. However, we identify two fundamental limitations. First, the optimal policy depends on arbitrary modeling choices (scalarization function, refe...

### 6. [SANet: A Semantic-aware Agentic AI Networking Framework for Cross-layer Optimization in 6G](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.22579)

**Authors**: Yong Xiao, Xubo Li, Haoran Zhou, Yingyu Li, Yayu Gao, Guangming Shi, Ping Zhang, Marwan Krunz  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-31  
**Score**: 5.5  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.22579v1  

#### Abstract
Agentic AI networking (AgentNet) is a novel AI-native networking paradigm in which a large number of specialized AI agents collaborate to perform autonomous decision-making, dynamic environmental adaptation, and complex missions. It has the potential to facilitate real-time network management and op...

## 4. å…³é”®ç»“è®ºå’Œå‘ç°

### 7. [SAMP-HDRL: Segmented Allocation with Momentum-Adjusted Utility for Multi-agent Portfolio Management via Hierarchical Deep Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.22895)

**Authors**: Xiaotian Ren, Nuerxiati Abudurexiti, Zhengyong Jiang, Angelos Stefanidis, Hongbin Liu, Jionglong Su  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-31  
**Score**: 5.5  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.22895v1  

#### Abstract
Portfolio optimization in non-stationary markets is challenging due to regime shifts, dynamic correlations, and the limited interpretability of deep reinforcement learning (DRL) policies. We propose a Segmented Allocation with Momentum-Adjusted Utility for Multi-agent Portfolio Management via Hierar...

### 8. [MindWatcher: Toward Smarter Multimodal Tool-Integrated Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.23412)

**Authors**: Jiawei Chen, Xintian Shen, Lihao Zheng, Zhenwei Shao, Hongyuan Zhang, Pengfei Yu, Xudong Rao, Ning Mao, Xiaobo Liu, Lian Wen, Chaoqun Du, Feng Gu, Wei He, Qizhen Li, Shanshan Li, Zide Liu, Jing Luo, Lifu Mu, Xuhao Pan, Chang Ren, Haoyi Sun, Qian Wang, Wei Wang, Hongfu Yang, Jiqing Zhan, Chunpeng Zhou, Zheng Zhou, Hao Ma, Tao Wei, Pan Zhou, Wei Chen  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-31  
**Score**: 5.0  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.23412v1  

#### Abstract
Traditional workflow-based agents exhibit limited intelligence when addressing real-world problems requiring tool invocation. Tool-integrated reasoning (TIR) agents capable of autonomous reasoning and tool invocation are rapidly emerging as a powerful approach for complex decision-making tasks invol...

## 4. å…³é”®ç»“è®ºå’Œå‘ç°

### 9. [HalluMat: Detecting Hallucinations in LLM-Generated Materials Science Content Through Multi-Stage Verification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.22396)

**Authors**: Bhanu Prakash Vangala, Sajid Mahmud, Pawan Neupane, Joel Selvaraj, Jianlin Cheng  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-31  
**Score**: 4.5  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.22396v1  

#### Abstract
Artificial Intelligence (AI), particularly Large Language Models (LLMs), is transforming scientific discovery, enabling rapid knowledge generation and hypothesis formulation. However, a critical challenge is hallucination, where LLMs generate factually incorrect or misleading information, compromisi...

#### ï¼ˆ3ï¼‰**Paraphrased Hallucination Consistency Score (PHCS)**

### 10. [Lightweight Inference-Time Personalization for Frozen Knowledge Graph Embeddings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.22398)

**Authors**: Ozan Oguztuzun, Cerag Oguztuzun  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-31  
**Score**: 4.5  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.22398v1  

#### Abstract
Foundation models for knowledge graphs (KGs) achieve strong cohort-level performance in link prediction, yet fail to capture individual user preferences; a key disconnect between general relational reasoning and personalized ranking. We propose GatedBias, a lightweight inference-time personalization...

## 1. è®ºæ–‡çš„ä¸»è¦è´¡çŒ®å’Œåˆ›æ–°ç‚¹

### è§£å†³çš„é—®é¢˜
ç°æœ‰çš„ **Knowledge Graph (KG)** åŸºç¡€æ¨¡å‹åœ¨ç¾¤ä½“å±‚é¢ï¼ˆcohort-levelï¼‰çš„é“¾æ¥é¢„æµ‹ä»»åŠ¡ä¸­è¡¨ç°ä¼˜å¼‚ï¼Œä½†åœ¨ä¸ªæ€§åŒ–æ¨èåœºæ™¯ä¸‹å­˜åœ¨æ˜æ˜¾ä¸è¶³ï¼š  
- åŒä¸€ä¸ªå€™é€‰å®ä½“å¯¹ä¸åŒç”¨æˆ·åº”æœ‰ä¸åŒçš„æ’åºï¼Œè€Œæ ‡å‡† KG æ¨¡å‹æ— æ³•æ•æ‰ä¸ªä½“ç”¨æˆ·çš„åå¥½ã€‚

### æå‡ºçš„æ–°æ–¹æ³•ï¼š**GatedBias**
ä½œè€…æå‡ºäº†ä¸€ç§è½»é‡çº§ã€ä»…åœ¨æ¨ç†é˜¶æ®µè¿›è¡Œä¸ªæ€§åŒ–çš„æ¡†æ¶ **GatedBias**ï¼Œç”¨äºä¸ºå†»ç»“çš„ KG åµŒå…¥æ·»åŠ ä¸ªæ€§åŒ–åç½®ï¼Œæ— éœ€æ›´æ–°ä¸»å¹²æ¨¡å‹å‚æ•°ã€‚

#### æ ¸å¿ƒæ€æƒ³ï¼š**Structure-Gated Adaptation**
- åˆ©ç”¨å›¾ç»“æ„ä¸­çš„äºŒå€¼é—¨æ§ï¼ˆbinary gatesï¼‰æ§åˆ¶ä¸ªæ€§åŒ–ä¿¡å·çš„å½±å“èŒƒå›´ã€‚
- å°†æ¯ä¸ªå°¾å®ä½“ $t$ æ˜ å°„åˆ°ä¸€ç»„ç»“æ„ç›¸å…³çš„å±æ€§ï¼ˆå¦‚ GENREã€AUTHOR ç­‰ï¼‰ï¼Œå½¢æˆ **gate vector** $g_k(t)$ï¼Œè¡¨ç¤ºè¯¥å®ä½“æ˜¯å¦å…·æœ‰æŸç±»å±æ€§ã€‚
- ç”¨æˆ·åå¥½ä»¥ç‰¹å¾å‘é‡ $f_k$ è¡¨ç¤ºï¼ˆä¾‹å¦‚åŸºäºäº¤äº’å†å²ç»Ÿè®¡çš„ genre é¢‘ç‡ï¼‰ã€‚
- æœ€ç»ˆçš„ä¸ªæ€§åŒ–åç½®å®šä¹‰ä¸ºï¼š
  $$
  b_p(t) = \sum_{k=1}^K \alpha_k \langle w_k, g_k(t) \odot f_k \rangle
  $$
  å…¶ä¸­ $\odot$ æ˜¯é€å…ƒç´ ä¹˜ç§¯ï¼Œ$w_k$ æ˜¯å°‘é‡å¯å­¦ä¹ æƒé‡ï¼Œ$\alpha_k$ æ˜¯ç¼©æ”¾å› å­ã€‚

#### åˆ›æ–°ç‚¹
1. **Post-hoc & Inference-Time Personalization**  
   ä¸ä¿®æ”¹é¢„è®­ç»ƒå¥½çš„ KG æ¨¡å‹ï¼ˆbackbone frozenï¼‰ï¼Œæ‰€æœ‰ä¸ªæ€§åŒ–æ“ä½œå‘ç”Ÿåœ¨æ¨ç†é˜¶æ®µï¼Œé¿å…é‡æ–°è®­ç»ƒã€‚
   
2. **ç»“æ„æ„ŸçŸ¥çš„å¯è§£é‡Šåç½®æœºåˆ¶ï¼ˆStructure-Gated Biasï¼‰**  
   åªæœ‰å½“å®ä½“å®é™…æ‹¥æœ‰æŸä¸ªå±æ€§æ—¶ï¼Œå¯¹åº”çš„ç”¨æˆ·åå¥½æ‰ä¼šè¢«æ¿€æ´»ï¼Œæå‡å¯è§£é‡Šæ€§å’Œæœ‰æ•ˆæ€§ã€‚

3. **æä½å‚æ•°å¼€é”€**  
   æ¯ä¸ªç”¨æˆ·ä»…éœ€çº¦ **~300 ä¸ªå¯è®­ç»ƒå‚æ•°**ï¼ˆè¿œå°äº backbone çš„æ•°åä¸‡å‚æ•°ï¼‰ï¼Œå®ç°é«˜æ•ˆéƒ¨ç½²ã€‚

4. **æå‡ºæ–°çš„è¯„ä¼°æŒ‡æ ‡**

   - **Counterfactual Responsiveness (CR)**ï¼šéªŒè¯ä¸ªæ€§åŒ–å“åº”æ˜¯å¦å…·å¤‡å› æœæ€§ï¼ˆå³å¢å¼ºæŸåå¥½ä¿¡å·åï¼Œç›¸å…³å®ä½“æ’åæ˜¯å¦æ˜¾è‘—ä¸Šå‡ï¼‰ã€‚

## 2. æ ¸å¿ƒå®éªŒæ–¹æ³•å’Œè®¾ç½®

### æ•°æ®é›†

#### Relation Group åˆ’åˆ†
- **Amazon-Book**:  
  - å†…å®¹åå¥½ç»„ï¼ˆPreferenceï¼‰: GENRE, THEME, SUBJECT, SERIES  
  - å…ƒæ•°æ®ç»„ï¼ˆMetadataï¼‰: AUTHOR, PUBLISHER, YEAR, LANGUAGE
- **Last-FM**:  
  - éŸ³ä¹åå¥½ç»„: GENRE, TAG, STYLE, MOOD, TEMPO, SIMILAR, INFLUENCED-BY ç­‰  
  - å…ƒæ•°æ®ç»„: LABEL, YEAR, COUNTRY, FORMAT, RELEASE DATE ç­‰

### å®éªŒè®¾ç½®
- **Backbone æ¨¡å‹**: ä½¿ç”¨é¢„è®­ç»ƒçš„ **DistMult** æ¨¡å‹ä½œä¸ºå†»ç»“ scorer $s_\theta(h,r,t)$ã€‚
- **ä¸ªæ€§åŒ–æ¨¡å—**: åœ¨æ¨ç†æ—¶å åŠ  GatedBias å¾—åˆ°æœ€ç»ˆå¾—åˆ†ï¼š
  $$
  s'(h,r,t) = s_\theta(h,r,t) + b_p(t)
  $$
- **è®­ç»ƒç›®æ ‡**: ä¼˜åŒ– hinge loss + æ­£åˆ™é¡¹ï¼ˆç¨€ç–æ€§å’Œç¨³å®šæ€§ï¼‰ï¼š
  $$
  \mathcal{L} = \sum_{(h,r,t)\in B} \max(0, 1 - [s'(h,r,t^+) - s'(h,r,t^-)]) + \lambda_1 \|w\|^2 + \lambda_2 \sum_k \alpha_k
  $$
- **ä¼˜åŒ–æ–¹å¼**: ä»…è®­ç»ƒ $w_k, \alpha_k$ï¼Œå…±çº¦ 292 ä¸ªå‚æ•°ï¼›batch size=4096ï¼Œlr=1e-3ï¼Œ5 epochsã€‚

### è¯„ä¼°æŒ‡æ ‡

#### æ ‡å‡†é“¾æ¥é¢„æµ‹æŒ‡æ ‡ï¼ˆç¡®ä¿ cohort æ€§èƒ½ä¸é€€åŒ–ï¼‰
- **MRR**, **Hits@k**, **NDCG@k**

#### æ–°æå‡ºçš„ä¸ªæ€§åŒ–ä¸“ç”¨æŒ‡æ ‡
1. **Alignment@k**
   - å®šä¹‰ï¼štop-k æ¨èä¸­â€œè¢«æ­£å‘æ¨åŠ¨ä¸”ä¸¤ç»„ç‰¹å¾å½±å“å·®å¼‚å¤§â€çš„å®ä½“æ¯”ä¾‹ã€‚
   - æ¡ä»¶ï¼š$ \max(c_A(t), c_B(t)) > 0 $ ä¸” $ |c_A(t) - c_B(t)| \geq T $
   - è¶Šé«˜è¶Šå¥½ï¼ˆâ†‘ï¼‰

2. **Counterfactual Responsiveness (CR)**
   - æ–¹æ³•ï¼šå°†æŸä¸€ç»„ç‰¹å¾ï¼ˆå¦‚ $f_A$ï¼‰æ”¾å¤§ $(1+\epsilon)$ å€ï¼ˆ$\epsilon=0.1$ï¼‰ï¼Œè§‚å¯Ÿå—ç›Šäºè¯¥ç»„çš„å®ä½“æ’åå˜åŒ–ã€‚
   - å®šä¹‰ï¼š
     $$
     CR_A = \mathbb{E}[\Delta \text{rank} \mid t^* \in A^+] - \mathbb{E}[\Delta \text{rank} \mid t^* \notin A^+]
     $$
   - è´Ÿå€¼è¡¨ç¤ºæ­£ç¡®å“åº”ï¼ˆè¶Šè´Ÿè¶Šå¥½ â†“ï¼‰

### åŸºçº¿æ–¹æ³•å¯¹æ¯”
| æ–¹æ³• | æè¿° |
|------|------|
| **Frozen Backbone (DistMult)** | æ— ä»»ä½•ä¸ªæ€§åŒ–ï¼ŒåŸºå‡†æ€§èƒ½ |
| **PatientNode** | æ¶ˆèå®éªŒï¼šä½¿ç”¨å›ºå®šå®ä½“åç½® MLPï¼Œå¿½ç•¥ç”¨æˆ· profile å’Œç»“æ„é—¨æ§ï¼ˆprofile-agnosticï¼‰ |

### 11. [Problems With Large Language Models for Learner Modelling: Why LLMs Alone Fall Short for Responsible Tutoring in K--12 Education](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.23036)

**Authors**: Danial Hooshyar, Yeongwook Yang, Gustav \v{S}\'i\v{r}, Tommi K\"arkk\"ainen, Raija H\"am\"al\"ainen, Mutlu Cukurova, Roger Azevedo  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-31  
**Score**: 4.5  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.23036v1  

#### Abstract
The rapid rise of large language model (LLM)-based tutors in K--12 education has fostered a misconception that generative models can replace traditional learner modelling for adaptive instruction. This is especially problematic in K--12 settings, which the EU AI Act classifies as high-risk domain re...

### 12. [Physics-Informed Neural Networks for Device and Circuit Modeling: A Case Study of NeuroSPICE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.23624)

**Authors**: Chien-Ting Tung, Chenming Hu  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-31  
**Score**: 4.5  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.23624v1  

#### Abstract
We present NeuroSPICE, a physics-informed neural network (PINN) framework for device and circuit simulation. Unlike conventional SPICE, which relies on time-discretized numerical solvers, NeuroSPICE leverages PINNs to solve circuit differential-algebraic equations (DAEs) by minimizing the residual o...

### 13. [Monadic Context Engineering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.22431)

**Authors**: Yifan Zhang, Mengdi Wang  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-31  
**Score**: 4.0  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.22431v1  

#### Abstract
The proliferation of Large Language Models (LLMs) has catalyzed a shift towards autonomous agents capable of complex reasoning and tool use. However, current agent architectures are frequently constructed using imperative, ad hoc patterns. This results in brittle systems plagued by difficulties in s...

# è®ºæ–‡æ€»ç»“ï¼š*Monadic Context Engineering*

## 1. è®ºæ–‡çš„ä¸»è¦è´¡çŒ®å’Œåˆ›æ–°ç‚¹

### è§£å†³çš„é—®é¢˜
å½“å‰åŸºäºå¤§è¯­è¨€æ¨¡å‹ï¼ˆLLMï¼‰çš„**AI Agent æ¶æ„**æ™®éé‡‡ç”¨**å‘½ä»¤å¼ã€ä¸´æ—¶æ‹¼å‡‘ï¼ˆad hocï¼‰çš„è®¾è®¡æ¨¡å¼**ï¼Œå¯¼è‡´ç³»ç»Ÿå­˜åœ¨ä»¥ä¸‹æ ¸å¿ƒç—›ç‚¹ï¼š
- **çŠ¶æ€ç®¡ç†å›°éš¾**ï¼šåœ¨å¤æ‚çš„æ¨ç†-è¡ŒåŠ¨å¾ªç¯ä¸­éš¾ä»¥å¯é åœ°ä¼ é€’è®°å¿†ã€ä¿¡å¿µå’Œå†å²ã€‚
- **é”™è¯¯å¤„ç†è„†å¼±**ï¼šAPI è¶…æ—¶ã€æ¨¡å‹è¾“å‡ºæ ¼å¼é”™è¯¯ç­‰ç°å®æ•…éšœå®¹æ˜“ç ´åæ•´ä¸ªæµç¨‹ï¼Œä¸”é”™è¯¯å¤„ç†é€»è¾‘æ±¡æŸ“ä¸»ä¸šåŠ¡ä»£ç ã€‚
- **å¹¶å‘ç¼–ç¨‹å¤æ‚**ï¼šå®ç°å¹¶è¡Œæ‰§è¡Œå¤šä¸ªå·¥å…·è°ƒç”¨æ—¶ï¼Œæ˜“é™·å…¥å›è°ƒåœ°ç‹±æˆ–æ‰‹åŠ¨çº¿ç¨‹ç®¡ç†çš„å¤æ‚æ€§ã€‚
- **ç¼ºä¹å¯ç»„åˆæ€§**ï¼šç»„ä»¶é—´é«˜åº¦è€¦åˆï¼Œéš¾ä»¥ç‹¬ç«‹æµ‹è¯•ã€å¤ç”¨å’Œé‡æ„ã€‚

è¿™äº›é—®é¢˜ä½¿å¾— Agent ç³»ç»Ÿ**éš¾ä»¥æµ‹è¯•ã€è°ƒè¯•å’Œæ‰©å±•**ï¼Œæˆä¸ºæ„å»ºé²æ£’ã€å¯æ‰©å±•æ™ºèƒ½ä½“çš„é‡å¤§éšœç¢ã€‚

### æå‡ºçš„æ–°æ–¹æ³•ä¸åˆ›æ–°æ€è·¯
æœ¬æ–‡æå‡º **Monadic Context Engineering (MCE)** â€”â€”ä¸€ç§å—å‡½æ•°å¼ç¼–ç¨‹å¯å‘çš„æ–°å‹ Agent æ¶æ„èŒƒå¼ï¼Œå…¶æ ¸å¿ƒæ˜¯åˆ©ç”¨èŒƒç•´è®ºä¸­çš„ä»£æ•°ç»“æ„ï¼ˆFunctor, Applicative Functor, Monadï¼‰ä¸º Agent è®¾è®¡æä¾›å½¢å¼åŒ–åŸºç¡€ã€‚

#### ä¸»è¦åˆ›æ–°ç‚¹åŒ…æ‹¬ï¼š
- **AgentMonad æŠ½è±¡**ï¼šè®¾è®¡äº†ä¸€ä¸ªåä¸º `AgentMonad` çš„å¤åˆå•å­ï¼ˆMonadï¼‰ï¼Œé€šè¿‡ **Monad Transformer Stack**ï¼ˆ`StateT S (EitherT E IO)`ï¼‰ç»Ÿä¸€ç®¡ç†ä¸‰å¤§æ ¸å¿ƒè®¡ç®—ä¸Šä¸‹æ–‡ï¼š
  - `IO` / `Task`ï¼šå¤„ç†å¤–éƒ¨å‰¯ä½œç”¨ï¼ˆå¦‚è°ƒç”¨ APIï¼‰
  - `EitherT`ï¼šå®ç°çŸ­è·¯å¼é”™è¯¯å¤„ç†ï¼ˆfailure short-circuitingï¼‰
  - `StateT`ï¼šè‡ªåŠ¨ä¼ é€’å†…éƒ¨çŠ¶æ€ï¼ˆmemory, historyï¼‰
- **å£°æ˜å¼å·¥ä½œæµ**ï¼šå¼€å‘è€…åªéœ€å®šä¹‰æ¯ä¸€æ­¥çš„çº¯é€»è¾‘å‡½æ•°ï¼Œé€šè¿‡ `bind`ï¼ˆ`.then()`ï¼‰æ“ä½œç¬¦é“¾å¼ç»„åˆï¼Œæ¡†æ¶è‡ªåŠ¨å¤„ç†çŠ¶æ€ä¼ é€’ã€é”™è¯¯ä¼ æ’­å’Œå¼‚æ­¥è°ƒåº¦ã€‚
- **Applicative å¹¶è¡Œæœºåˆ¶**ï¼šå¼•å…¥ `gather` æ“ä½œç¬¦ï¼Œæ”¯æŒå¯¹ç‹¬ç«‹ä»»åŠ¡è¿›è¡ŒçœŸæ­£çš„å¹¶è¡Œæ‰§è¡Œï¼Œæ˜¾è‘—æå‡ I/O å¯†é›†å‹ä»»åŠ¡çš„æ•ˆç‡ã€‚

### 14. [DICE: Discrete Interpretable Comparative Evaluation with Probabilistic Scoring for Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.22629)

**Authors**: Shiyan Liu, Jian Ma, Rui Qu  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-31  
**Score**: 4.0  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.22629v1  

#### Abstract
As Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) systems evolve toward more sophisticated architectures, ensuring their trustworthiness through explainable and robust evaluation becomes critical. Existing scalar metrics suffer from limited interpretability, inadequate uncertainty quantification, and computat...

## 1. è®ºæ–‡çš„ä¸»è¦è´¡çŒ®å’Œåˆ›æ–°ç‚¹

### è§£å†³çš„é—®é¢˜
å½“å‰å¯¹ **Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG)** ç³»ç»Ÿçš„è¯„ä¼°å­˜åœ¨ä»¥ä¸‹å…³é”®æŒ‘æˆ˜ï¼š
- **å¯è§£é‡Šæ€§å·®**ï¼šä¼ ç»Ÿæ ‡é‡æŒ‡æ ‡ï¼ˆå¦‚ BLEUã€ROUGEã€RAGASï¼‰ä»…æä¾›å•ä¸€åˆ†æ•°ï¼Œæ— æ³•è¯´æ˜â€œä¸ºä½•ä¸€ä¸ªç³»ç»Ÿä¼˜äºå¦ä¸€ä¸ªâ€ã€‚
- **ä¸ç¡®å®šæ€§é‡åŒ–ä¸è¶³**ï¼šå¤šæ•°è‡ªåŠ¨è¯„ä¼°æ–¹æ³•ç¼ºä¹å¯¹åˆ¤æ–­ç½®ä¿¡åº¦çš„å»ºæ¨¡ï¼Œéš¾ä»¥åæ˜ è¯„ä¼°æœ¬èº«çš„å¯é æ€§ã€‚
- **è®¡ç®—æ•ˆç‡ä½**ï¼šåœ¨å¤šç³»ç»Ÿæ¯”è¾ƒä¸­ï¼Œå…¨é…å¯¹æ¯”è¾ƒï¼ˆexhaustive pairwiseï¼‰å¤æ‚åº¦ä¸º $O(N^2)$ï¼Œæˆæœ¬é«˜æ˜‚ã€‚
- **é²æ£’æ€§å¼±**ï¼šLLM-as-a-judge æ–¹æ³•æ˜“å—æç¤ºæ•æ„Ÿæ€§å’Œä½ç½®åå·®å½±å“ã€‚

è¿™äº›é—®é¢˜é˜»ç¢äº† RAG æŠ€æœ¯åœ¨é‡‘èã€æ³•å¾‹ç­‰é«˜é£é™©é¢†åŸŸçš„å¯ä¿¡éƒ¨ç½²ã€‚

### æå‡ºçš„æ–°æ–¹æ³•ï¼šDICE æ¡†æ¶
ä½œè€…æå‡º **DICE**ï¼ˆDiscrete Interpretable Comparative Evaluationï¼‰ï¼Œä¸€ç§ä¸¤é˜¶æ®µã€è¯æ®è€¦åˆçš„è¯„ä¼°æ¡†æ¶ï¼Œæ ¸å¿ƒåˆ›æ–°å¦‚ä¸‹ï¼š

#### ï¼ˆ1ï¼‰**ä¸¤é˜¶æ®µè¯„ä¼°æœºåˆ¶**
- **Stage I: Evidence-Coupled Deep Analysis**
  - åˆ¤æ–­æ¨¡å‹åŸºäºæ£€ç´¢åˆ°çš„ä¸Šä¸‹æ–‡ï¼ˆcontextï¼‰ã€ç”Ÿæˆç­”æ¡ˆï¼ˆanswerï¼‰å’Œæ ‡å‡†äº‹å®ï¼ˆgroundtruthï¼‰è¿›è¡Œæ·±åº¦åˆ†æã€‚
  - è¾“å‡ºé€æ˜çš„ **Chain of Thought æ¨ç†é“¾**ï¼Œæ˜ç¡®æŒ‡å‡ºæ¯ä¸ªç³»ç»Ÿçš„ä¼˜åŠ£ï¼ˆå¦‚æ˜¯å¦å‡†ç¡®ã€å®Œæ•´ã€ç›¸å…³ï¼‰ã€‚
  - æ”¯æŒç³»ç»Ÿæ€§é”™è¯¯è¯Šæ–­ä¸å¯æ“ä½œæ”¹è¿›å»ºè®®ã€‚

- **Stage II: Probabilistic Confidence-Aware Scoring**
  - åŸºäºç¬¬ä¸€é˜¶æ®µçš„åˆ¤æ–­è¾“å‡ºï¼ˆå• token: `A`, `B`, `Tie`ï¼‰ï¼Œæå–å…¶ logits å¹¶é€šè¿‡ softmax è½¬æ¢ä¸ºæ¦‚ç‡åˆ†å¸ƒã€‚
  - å¼•å…¥ **æ¦‚ç‡é—´éš”ï¼ˆprobability marginï¼‰** $\Delta P = P_{\text{max}} - P_{\text{second}}$ æ¥è¡¡é‡åˆ¤æ–­ç½®ä¿¡åº¦ã€‚
  - æ ¹æ®ç½®ä¿¡åº¦é‡‡ç”¨ä¸åŒè¯„åˆ†ç­–ç•¥ï¼š
    - é«˜ç½®ä¿¡ï¼ˆ$\Delta P \geq 0.1$ï¼‰ï¼šç¡¬è¯„åˆ†ï¼ˆHard Scoringï¼‰
    - ä½ç½®ä¿¡ï¼ˆ$\Delta P < 0.1$ï¼‰ï¼šè½¯è¯„åˆ†ï¼ˆSoft Scoringï¼‰ï¼Œå°† tie æ¦‚ç‡æŒ‰æ¯”ä¾‹åˆ†é…ç»™ A/Bã€‚

#### ï¼ˆ2ï¼‰**é«˜æ•ˆå¤šç³»ç»Ÿæ’åæœºåˆ¶ï¼šSwiss-system Tournament**
- é‡‡ç”¨ç‘å£«åˆ¶é”¦æ ‡èµ›ç»„ç»‡å¤šç³»ç»Ÿæ¯”è¾ƒï¼Œé¿å… $O(N^2)$ å…¨é…å¯¹ã€‚
- åŠ¨æ€åŒ¹é… Elo åˆ†ç›¸è¿‘çš„ç³»ç»Ÿï¼Œæ¯è½®æ›´æ–° Elo å¾—åˆ†ã€‚

### 15. [Divergent-Convergent Thinking in Large Language Models for Creative Problem Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.23601)

**Authors**: Manh Hung Nguyen, Adish Singla  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-31  
**Score**: 4.0  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.23601v1  

#### Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) have significant potential for generating educational questions and problems, enabling educators to create large-scale learning materials. However, LLMs are fundamentally limited by the ``Artificial Hivemind'' effect, where they generate similar responses within the same...

## 1. è®ºæ–‡çš„ä¸»è¦è´¡çŒ®å’Œåˆ›æ–°ç‚¹

### è§£å†³çš„é—®é¢˜
å¤§å‹è¯­è¨€æ¨¡å‹ï¼ˆLLMsï¼‰åœ¨ç”Ÿæˆæ•™è‚²ç±»é—®é¢˜ï¼ˆå¦‚ç¼–ç¨‹é¢˜ã€æ•°å­¦é¢˜ç­‰ï¼‰æ–¹é¢å±•ç°å‡ºå·¨å¤§æ½œåŠ›ï¼Œä½†å­˜åœ¨â€œ**Artificial Hivemind**â€æ•ˆåº”â€”â€”å³åŒä¸€æ¨¡å‹å†…éƒ¨è¾“å‡ºé‡å¤ã€ä¸åŒæ¨¡å‹ä¹‹é—´è¾“å‡ºè¶‹åŒï¼Œå¯¼è‡´ç”Ÿæˆçš„é—®é¢˜ç¼ºä¹å¤šæ ·æ€§ä¸åˆ›é€ æ€§ã€‚è¿™ç§ç°è±¡é™åˆ¶äº†å­¦ç”Ÿæ¥è§¦å¤šæ ·åŒ–æ€ç»´çš„æœºä¼šï¼Œå½±å“åˆ›é€ åŠ›åŸ¹å…»ã€‚

### ç›¸æ¯”ç°æœ‰æ–¹æ³•çš„ä¼˜åŠ¿

## ğŸš€ How to Use

1. **Fork this repository** to your GitHub account
2. **Customize the configuration** by editing `config.json`:
   - Add/remove arXiv categories (e.g., `cs.AI`, `cs.LG`, `cs.CL`)
   - Modify keywords to match your research interests
   - Adjust `max_papers` and `days_back` settings
3. **Enable GitHub Actions** in your repository settings
4. **The bot will automatically run daily** and update the README.md

## ğŸ“ Customization

### arXiv Categories
Common categories include:

- `cs.LG` - Machine Learning

- `cs.CV` - Computer Vision
- `cs.NE` - Neural and Evolutionary Computing
- `stat.ML` - Machine Learning (Statistics)

### Keywords
Add keywords that match your research interests. The bot will search for these terms in paper titles and abstracts.

### Exclude Keywords
Add terms to exclude certain types of papers (e.g., "survey", "review", "tutorial").
